National Society, Oslo, June 24: The famous Norwegian Arctic exploration ship William Booths struck ice and sank 2,450 miles from Greenland. Fourteen crew members were buried at sea.

Southern Cross Encounter

Regulations for the National Internal Affairs Conference 2

It has been decided that the National Internal Affairs Conference will be held in Beijing on October 1st of this year. All conference regulations and rules of procedure have been drafted by the Ministry of Internal Affairs and submitted to the government for approval and record. The conference regulations are recorded below: (Article 1) The Ministry of Internal Affairs, in order to rigorously implement political tutelage, unify internal affairs administration, and solicit opinions from all parties, specially convenes the National Internal Affairs Conference. (Article 2) All external correspondence of this conference shall be conducted in the name of the Ministry of Internal Affairs. (Article 3) This conference shall be organized by the following members: (1) Each provincial government shall send one representative. Provincial government representatives shall be limited to members of the provincial government, but may bring two important officials to attend as observers. (2) Each municipal government directly under the Executive Yuan shall send one representative. Municipal government representatives shall be limited to officials above the level of bureau director, but may bring two important officials to attend as observers. (3) Each ministry related to internal affairs shall temporarily select one representative. (4) The Ministry of Internal Affairs shall select and hire five experts. (5) The Minister, Vice Minister, Counselors, Department Directors, and Senior Secretaries of the Ministry of Internal Affairs. (6) The Chief of the Capital Police Department. (Article 4) When discussing matters at this conference, the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Examination Yuan, and the Control Yuan shall be requested to send personnel to participate and provide guidance. (Article 5) If the experts hired by the Ministry of Internal Affairs overlap with the representatives of the National Government or various Yuan, Ministries, and Commissions, the Ministry of Internal Affairs may hire additional personnel to supplement them. (Article 6) This conference shall have one chairman and two vice-chairmen. The chairman shall be the Minister of Internal Affairs, and the vice-chairmen shall be the Vice Ministers. (Article 7) This conference shall be held in the capital, scheduled to begin on October 1st of the 19th year. (Article 8) The scope of proposals for this conference shall be as follows: (1) Those submitted by the Ministry of Internal Affairs for discussion. (2) Those proposed by attending members or those made as temporary motions. (3) Suggestions from various organizations introduced with the joint signatures of three or more members. (Article 9) This conference may only convene if more than half of the members have reported their attendance. (Article 10) If a member of this conference has a proposal, it must be submitted to the secretariat of this conference seven days before the opening of the conference so that it can be included in the agenda. Any temporary proposal must be submitted in writing to the chairman of this conference with the co-signature of ten or more members for consideration and inclusion in the agenda. Any temporary motion must be seconded by three or more members and approved by the chairman before it can become a formal proposal. (Article 11) Any proposal of this conference that needs to be reviewed shall be reviewed by a review committee organized by members designated by the chairman. (Article 12) The decisions made by this conference shall be adopted and implemented by the Ministry of Internal Affairs. (Article 13) The secretariat of this conference shall be responsible for various affairs, and its regulations shall be determined separately. (Article 14) The travel expenses of the members of this conference shall be borne by their respective localities, but the board and lodging during the conference shall be provided by this conference. (Article 15) All expenses of this conference shall be budgeted by the Ministry of Internal Affairs and submitted for approval. After the conference is completed, a final account shall be compiled and submitted for verification. (Article 16) If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they shall be amended by the Ministry of Internal Affairs. (Article 17) These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Zhang Guijun's Counterattack on Youxian Fails 3

After Jiang and Cai's divisions captured Youxian, they advanced towards Liling and Pingxiang. Huang Shaoxiong's troops were defeated by Jiang's division in Changning. According to a Guangzhou dispatch, after the Eighth Route Army poured into Hunan, Zhang Guijun was attacked from both sides in Changsha, Yueyang and was forced to withdraw from Changsha. A portion planned to return from Liling to counterattack Youxian. At the same time, Huang Shaoxiong's troops, who were lingering on the Guilin border, attempted to sneak into Changning from Lingling to try to cut off the rear of Hengzhou. Fierce battles have been taking place in the Youxian area since the 17th. It is reported that the enemy troops are a certain unit of the Gui Army, which launched a fierce attack on the Shen Guanghan brigade and the Pi Cai division training regiment in Youxian. Cai's division launched three assaults on Youxian before defeating the enemy, who retreated towards Zhuting and Xinshi. Cai's division estimated on the 18th that the enemy in Youxian was still trying to hold firm, with the appearance of entering Pingxiang. Therefore, after Cai's division of the Eighth Route Army captured Youxian from the right, Jiang Guangnai's division from Hengshan also detoured from Youxian, concentrating the Guo Enyan regiment and the Hua Zhenzhong and Zhang Shide brigades to Youxian. Immediately, they searched and suppressed the area towards Zhushi, Xinting and Liling. Recently, the second batch of troops arriving in Chenzhou, the Zhang Li regiment, the Fan Dexing regiment and the Wang Dinghua regiment, have been marching to Youxian at full speed in order to take over the defense of Youxian, so that the Jiang and Cai divisions on the front line can pursue Liling. At the same time, Li Yangjing's division and Huang Yanzhen's brigade, which were going to Xiangtan on the left, did not encounter any fighting due to the rapid retreat of Zhang Guijun's troops in Xiangtan. On the 19th, they continued to advance from Xiaohuashi to Huangmao. It is expected that they will meet with the Jiang and Cai troops advancing towards Liling during the day to encircle and annihilate the remaining enemies. As for the southern Hunan area, the military situation in Changning has also been quite smooth recently. Huang Shaoxiong, who was recently in Lingling, sent Huang Xuchu's troops, about two to three thousand men, into Changning on the 17th. Jiang Guangnai, hearing the news at the front, immediately sent a regiment from Li's division and a regiment from the division south along Baifang to meet and engage Huang's troops in a fierce battle for half a day. At the same time, the Yue Shao Pass Headquarters also sent four aircraft from Nanhai, Guangzhou, Panyu and Zhujiang to the Changning front to bomb the enemy. At noon on the 18th, the four aircraft circled in the sky and dropped bombs, and the enemy began to flee in panic. The Shao Pass Headquarters received a telegram from Jiang Guangnai yesterday reporting that [the Guangzhou aircraft landed five miles away from our army's position in Changning. The aircraft was slightly damaged, but the personnel are safe. The enemy troops in Changning have been defeated by our army. Signed, Jiang Guangnai, at Shenke]. Since the enemy troops in southern Hunan have been defeated, the Eighth Route Army will drive north to Liling and Pingxiang. Chen Jitang, the commander-in-chief of the Eighth Route Army, has made a special trip to Hunan and arrived in Yizhang with the headquarters staff on the 20th. He will arrive in Chenzhou tomorrow. (June 21st)

Lu Dipin to Depart to Supervise the Troops 4

Zhang Huizan Will Also Accompany Him

A dispatch from Nanchang on the 21st reports that after the order for the general offensive against Zhang Guijun was issued, the Zhang Huizan and Jin Handing divisions of the Ninth Route Army had already advanced to the Ping, Liu, Li and Zhu areas in Hunan. It is now reported that Lu Dipin, the commander-in-chief of the Ninth Route Army, decided to depart for southern Hunan within the next few days to supervise the troops, as Zhang Guijun's remnants were scurrying around everywhere after withdrawing from Changsha. Zhang Huizan, the division commander, will also accompany him. He is currently preparing everything. Yesterday, General Commander Lu telegraphed Chairman Jiang and President Tan, requesting them to appoint someone to act as chairman or to be appointed by the provincial government to take over the important post. Once the National Government's reply arrives, he will be able to depart. General Commander Lu also sent his aide-de-camp, Cao Xinbiao, to Beijing a few days ago to pay respects to Tan Yankai, the acting chairman of the National Government, and Zhu Peiting, the acting commander-in-chief, to report on the progress of the Ninth Route Army's divisions, request instructions on everything, and receive military pay, firearms and all military supplies. Cao has already completed his mission and returned to the province yesterday. According to him, the battles on the Longhai and Pinghan lines are extremely smooth. Recently, several new divisions have been added, and their strength is becoming more and more powerful. As for the Ninth Route Army's monthly expenses, they are set at 30,000 yuan, and temporary expenses can be requested at any time. Furthermore, Lu telegraphed He Jian on the 18th to congratulate him on the recapture of Changsha and ordered the Jin and Zhang divisions to quickly join forces with the Sixth and Eighth Route Armies in Liling and Liuyang to encircle and suppress Zhang Guijun's remnants.

Xuzhou Garrison Command 5

Promulgates Martial Law Regulations Effective Officially Starting from the 21st

A dispatch from Xuzhou states that the Xuzhou Garrison Headquarters, considering Xuzhou to be a vital hub on the Jinpu and Longhai railways and a gathering place for people from all directions, and at this time of war, in order to consolidate the rear defense, it is imperative to declare martial law. Having submitted a request to Director He of the Xuzhou Headquarters and received approval, martial law was officially declared starting from the 21st, and ten articles of martial law regulations were formulated and promulgated for implementation. (1) The hours from 12:00 noon to 4:00 AM the following morning are designated as martial law hours, and pedestrian traffic is prohibited. (2) Assemblies, associations, speeches, newspapers, magazines, cartoons, slogans, advertisements, etc. that may hinder the revolutionary military effort or exhibit counter-revolutionary sentiments are prohibited. (3) Public riots, strikes, and market boycotts that directly or indirectly hinder the revolutionary military effort and local security are prohibited. (4) The export of goods needed for military supplies may be prohibited as necessary. (5) Private firearms, ammunition, weapons, fire tools, and all dangerous items will be inspected and may be seized or confiscated as necessary. (6) Postal, telegraph, and other communication agencies must be closely monitored and inspected. Unauthorized private coded communications will be detained. (7) Troops will be stationed at train stations, ships, and various checkpoints and strategic locations to conduct inspections. (8) When necessary, with the permission of the highest-ranking officer, homes, buildings, vehicles, and ships may be searched. (9) During martial law hours, passage is not permitted without a permit. (10) All entertainment venues must cease operations during martial law hours. (June 21st)

Case of French Sailors Shooting and Wounding Chinese Police 6

French Consul in Hankou Files a Counter-Protest

Municipal Government Prepares a Serious Refutation

A dispatch from Hankou reports that in the case of French sailors stationed in Hankou shooting and wounding Chinese police officer Liu Jinshan on the 14th of this month, the Hankou Municipal Government has made serious representations to the French Consul in Hankou. Yesterday, the 23rd, the municipal government received a reply from French Consul Berthes, not only denying that there was a shooting of a Chinese police officer, but also protesting to the municipal government that the detention of French officer Ge Qing by the Chinese police station was detrimental to the treaty. It is heard that the municipal government has now decided to issue a serious refutation to clarify the responsibility. The original letter from the French Consul is recorded below: [In reply:] I acknowledge receipt of your esteemed letter of yesterday and understand its contents. In order to continue the negotiations between the two parties on Sunday of last week and the letter given to you at that time, this consul makes a serious protest to your mayor regarding the handling of the incident by the 11th Precinct on the night of the 14th. The reason why this consul is firm on this point and repeatedly discusses it is that the responsible authorities of your country seem to have forgotten to fulfill the various treaties signed between China and France. French residents should be tried by the French authorities, especially naval crew members. Therefore, the responsibility of the Public Security Bureau authorities should be to immediately transfer the sailors to their officers, and the officers should transfer them to their ship captain, in accordance with the treaties between our two countries. Even if the perpetrator of the incident is apprehended, this should be done in this way. However, it was necessary for this consul to contact you late at night to prove the innocence of naval officer Mr. Ge Qing before he could be released. As for the facts, the captains of the two warships anchored in this port have already joined this consul in a detailed investigation of the matter. The details are as follows: (1) Naval officer Mr. Ge Qing was originally on the "Martyr" warship. After the captain received news of the incident, Mr. Ge Qing was ordered by the captain, along with another colleague, to go to the scene of the incident to investigate and verify that the muzzle of his gun did not match the fired bullet. (2) French sailors cannot be held responsible for the indiscriminate firing of guns on Er Yao Road. French sailors are absolutely prohibited from carrying firearms when they go ashore. Moreover, the chief of the 11th Precinct personally witnessed and searched the body at the Palermo Cafe, which can be used as evidence that French sailors did not fire guns illegally. Only someone reported to you that only French sailors were on the street at the time of the incident. It is not difficult for this report to be shown to you to be inaccurate. It is known that a sailor from another country was also injured on this street, indicating that there were not only French sailors on the street. This consul does not need to point out who it is, but cannot listen to rumors that disturb people's hearing. (3) The two French gunners in the Mengduo Cafe were also arrested and taken to the 11th Precinct when they went out. They were not only tied up, but also abused. It is feared that they did not report to the precinct chief when they were detained here. A doctor's explanation is attached for reference. Furthermore, this consul must inform you that this is absolutely someone falsely identifying Mr. Ge Qing as the gun-firing murderer, inciting the police and the public with lies, and deceiving the 11th Precinct chief, so that the police and judicial authorities were led astray on an erroneous path from the beginning. French sailors were detained for several hours, and French military officers were detained for even longer, just like other criminals, and then violence was inflicted on two French sailors who had absolutely nothing to do with the matter, which is extremely inappropriate. I hereby send this letter to your mayor for your investigation and consideration. (1) An apology should be made to the commander of our country's navy regarding the insult to the French naval officer and French sailors. (2) The perpetrator of the crime should be punished. As for whether our government will have other demands in the future, this consul will first reserve all rights. This consul and the captain of our country's "Martyr" warship are extremely grateful for the meeting you granted at one o'clock the previous night. I hereby express my gratitude and wish you good health.

Guangdong Province Clears Out Bandits in Various Subordinate Areas 7

The Provincial Government Lists the Names of Bandit Lairs and Bandit Leaders

Orders the Department of Civil Affairs to Instruct Various Counties to Annihilate Them Within a Time Limit

A dispatch from Guangzhou reports that Guangdong Province recently, with the war still ongoing and the Gui situation just settled, has again successively transferred large numbers of troops to Hunan Province. During this period of troop movements, the defense arrangements were temporarily incomplete, or the incoming troops failed to succeed the outgoing troops seamlessly. At times, there may be vacuums in the local areas, and bandits lurking in the mountains may rise up and cause trouble, harming the villages. The authorities have recently received numerous reports of banditry from various places and have strictly ordered local officials to earnestly and thoroughly suppress the bandits to eliminate the people's suffering. It is found that the most rampant banditry recently is in Dongjiang. Because the subordinate areas of Dongjiang have suffered consecutive years of disaster, the remnants of the bandits are lurking. Once the government troops are transferred, they will come out and cause disturbances. Moreover, the terrain of Dongjiang borders on Fujian and Jiangxi, making it easier for bandit parties to enter and exit. Recently, after the Jiang Division of the Dongjiang Defense Army was transferred to Hunan, the bandits in the Chao and Mei areas took advantage of the opportunity before Xiang Hanping's troops could take over. For example, Jiaoling, a subordinate area of Mei, has recently been invaded by communist bandits from Wuping and Yanqian on the Fujian border. The county magistrate of Xunwu County on the Jiangxi border has even fled to Jiaoling with his staff. Moreover, Shekeng in Mei County has been raided by bandits from Raoping, and the post has also been robbed. Bingcun was besieged by bandits several times on the 4th. Kuitan near Haifeng has recently reported repeated bandit alarms. In addition, pirates in the five counties of Nanhai, Panyu, Dongguan, Shunde and Zhongshan under the Guangzhou Prefecture are rampant, obstructing waterways and robbing villages and ferries from time to time. Especially in Zhongshan County, the subordinate area has recently suffered the most from bandit disasters. The provincial government has received repeated reports and has ordered the relevant authorities to investigate the places where the bandits gather and list the names of the bandit gangs. In addition to consulting with the military authorities and ordering the defense army to suppress them, it has also ordered the Department of Civil Affairs to instruct the various counties to cooperate with the police teams to earnestly suppress the bandits in order to reassure the people. The original order stated: "It is found that the areas of Sanshan, Zidong, Jili and Huangguajiao in Nanhai County; Shibi, Shenyong and Motiedie of Panyu; Juhuawan, Heqian, Ganzhutan, Guohai, Huoshaotou, Banshawei and Yinggejui of Shunde County; Baihuatou and Baigongsha of Zhongshan County; Daojiao, Zhangpeng and Hongwuwu of Dongguan County; Lanwei, Dushu, Laoshushi, Yuezhang, Xiancun and Tuqian of Dongjiang County are all areas where bandits frequently appear. Orders have been issued repeatedly for clearing and suppression. Recently, bandit leaders Luo Ji Hong, Chen Shiyao, Zhang Dingji, Zhang Ru, He Fei, Lei Gongquan, Tang Lai, Chen Duanmin, He Ran, He Yu, Liao Liu, Liang Sao, Liang Xiang, Deng Han, Yiya Zai, Chen Dizai, Yuan Doupi, Yuan Da Zeng, Luo Bu Xu Zhendong Guan Hong and others have taken advantage of the troop transfers and departures to loot and bomb ferries on a large scale. Such rampant harm is extremely serious and should be severely suppressed to maintain security. In addition to requesting Commander-in-Chief Chen to dispatch troops to the counties of Nanfan, Zhongshun and Dong to assist the counties in clearing them within a time limit, please also request Commander Chen of the Navy to consider the situation and dispatch patrol ships to station at the key points of each river and order the ships in each section to patrol carefully and protect them effectively. It is still necessary to cooperate with the battalions and counties to block and intercept the bandits in order to advance by both land and water and clear them as soon as possible. The director of the department is also ordered to strictly order the magistrates of the above-mentioned counties to mobilize the entire county's corps police force to meet with the fleet and properly formulate a joint suppression plan, dividing the troops and launching attacks within a specified period of one month to annihilate all bandit gangs and ensure the safety of travelers. The department shall also report the compliance situation at any time for inspection. There shall be no delays. The district and township police teams in the counties along the river have the responsibility to protect the local area. In the future, if there are any bombings of ferries in the section, and they fail to provide immediate assistance or fail to solve the case afterwards, how should they be severely punished to serve as a warning? The department shall also formulate a proper plan for presentation and compliance."

The Phenomenon of Finance in Shanxi Province 8

A dispatch from Taiyuan reports that there are generally three types of banknotes circulating in this province: Shanxi Provincial Bank banknotes, Bank of China banknotes, and private banknotes issued by merchants in various counties and cities. Bank of China banknotes declined sharply two years ago. Although the bank still maintains a branch in Taiyuan, it is only to maintain appearances. The issuance of private banknotes by merchants in various counties and cities is rampant. The face value of the banknotes ranges from as high as several tens of yuan to as low as five copper coins. The exchange rate of private banknotes for one silver dollar varies greatly, with some requiring more than ten thousand and others requiring six or seven thousand. Moreover, these private banknotes have no guarantee whatsoever. Every time they are moved to another county, they become worthless paper. In recent years, the losses suffered by people in various counties from these private banknotes have been enormous, and the financial system of the entire province has been disrupted and harmed. Last year, the Department of Civil Affairs and the Department of Finance jointly issued an order to the counties, ordering the merchants to recall the private banknotes they had issued in three phases and destroy them. The third phase is about to expire, and the results are still considerable. It is expected that they will be able to be completely recalled in the near future. At present, the only banknotes circulating throughout the province are those of the Provincial Bank. There are two types of Provincial Bank banknotes: silver dollar banknotes and copper coin banknotes. The lowest denomination of silver banknotes is one jiao, and the highest is one hundred yuan. The lowest denomination of copper coin banknotes is ten coins, and the highest is one hundred coins. A year ago, the exchange rate of Provincial Bank banknotes for one silver dollar was only a few copper coins, and the remittance fee was an average of twenty or thirty yuan per thousand yuan. The exchange rate of copper coins for one silver dollar was an average of three hundred and sixty or seventy coins, and the exchange rate of copper coin banknotes for one silver dollar was an average of four hundred coins or so. After Yan Xishan and Li Bing went to Zhengzhou last year to supervise the troops during the campaign against Tang Shengzhi, unscrupulous merchants in Taiyuan engaged in large-scale speculation, raised remittance fees, and manipulated the price of Provincial Bank banknotes, causing the

Page 10

June 26, 1930 (Shen Bao Third Sheet) Thursday

Price of Provincial Bank banknotes to fall to around 70% of its face value. For a time, the entire city was in a state of panic. Later, Yan returned from Zhengzhou and strongly advocated redemption, and the market began to stabilize slightly. Since the opening of redemption, a total of four to five million yuan was redeemed in less than ten days. Because unscrupulous merchants were transporting the redeemed silver dollars to the provincial government to buy banknotes and then transporting them to the province for redemption in order to make a profit, and some even buried the silver dollars underground and did not use them again, the original purpose of opening redemption was greatly lost. Therefore, the authorities resolutely stopped redemption again. Since then, the price of Provincial Bank banknotes has not been able to recover to the level of a year ago. When the recent war broke out, Provincial Bank banknotes fell sharply again. A week ago, one yuan of Provincial Bank banknotes fell to only five or six jiao. The prices of all goods in the market rose several times, and the people were in dire straits. The provincial government then ordered five agencies, including the Department of Finance and the Military Police Headquarters, to establish a remittance inspection committee to implement remittance inspection and restrict the outflow of silver dollars to stabilize remittance fees. The current remittance inspection committee stipulates that the remittance fee is 300 yuan per thousand yuan, but unscrupulous merchants still often comply with the regulations in appearance but violate them in reality. The prices of goods are still rising, but the people's morale in the market has greatly stabilized compared to before. Silver banknotes are no longer a major problem. The only problem is copper coin banknotes. The Department of Finance previously stipulated that the exchange rate of copper coin banknotes for silver dollars was 400 coins per yuan. This has been implemented smoothly for several months. The crux of the current problem is the exchange of copper coin banknotes for small change. Because there have been more copper coins than copper coin banknotes in this province for many years, the Department of Finance printed one million new copper coin banknotes last month and issued them to the Provincial Bank for use. Recently, the number of copper coin banknotes in the market has increased sharply, and the number of copper coins has been decreasing day by day. The lowest denomination of copper coin banknotes is ten coins, and there are often disputes and friction between shops in transactions due to the exchange of small change. This phenomenon has almost spread throughout the province. The Provincial Bank has previously reported this situation to the Department of Finance. Now the Department of Finance has formulated three measures for the exchange of copper coin banknotes and announced them for implementation in order to provide relief. This also shows the financial problems of this province. The exchange measures are appended below: (1) Anyone who comes to the bank to exchange up to 100 copper coin banknotes or 3 jiao of silver dollar banknotes will be paid 10 copper coins and the rest will be paid with the bank's copper coin banknotes or silver jiao banknotes (for example, if you hold a 10-coin banknote to exchange, you will be paid entirely with copper coins; if you hold a 20-coin banknote to exchange, you will be paid with half of the number and the rest by analogy). (2) Anyone who comes to the bank to exchange more than 100 copper coin banknotes or more than 3 jiao of silver dollar banknotes will be paid with one-tenth of the number of copper coins, but no matter how many silver or copper coin banknotes you exchange, you will not be paid more than 100 copper coins. The rest will be paid with the bank's copper coin banknotes or silver jiao banknotes. (3) Each person may not have more than two exchanges of copper coins per day. If there are more than two exchanges, they may be rejected.

Twists and Turns in the CER Electrical Rights Conference 9

Final Opinion of the Communications Committee

Li Shaogeng Decides to Mediate 10

A dispatch from Harbin on the 20th reports that Li Deyan, the Deputy Director of the Postal and Communications Department of the Chinese Eastern Railway (CER), returned to Harbin on the 18th of this month after requesting instructions from Liaoning on the 17th. Mr. Li notified the Russian Chairman Jenissoff, requesting to continue negotiations and scheduled a meeting at the Railway Bureau on the afternoon of the 19th. The Russian side did not reply that night, so the meeting on the 19th did not succeed. Yesterday, Li went to see the Chinese representative and the Director-General of the Railway, Li Shaogeng, to deliver the Communications Committee's opinions on the CER electrical rights conference. Because the Russian Chairman went to Liaoning to attend the second anniversary of Zhang Zuolin's death, Li Shaogeng will mediate after his return to Harbin to bring the opinions of both sides closer. Then, a special committee will be convened to negotiate the contract terms and submit them to the General Assembly for approval. Jenissoff is scheduled to return to Harbin on the 24th. It is still difficult to predict whether this matter can be remedied during the exchange of opinions. It is heard that the Communications Committee's opinions are about four items, all of which concern international telecommunications and official electrical rights. The commercial electrical dispute has been deliberately abandoned. Therefore, it is said that this is an exchange of views, but it is better to say that it is a last resort and concession. Perhaps the Russian side, seeing that the conditions are not too harsh, will allow the conference to continue. It is also heard that the Communications Committee has planned that if the Russian side insists on its own opinions and only seeks to benefit its own side, the Communications Committee will no longer proceed with the conference and will directly announce that the old contract signed in 1922 is invalid. This measure is based on the 1922 old contract [If either party deems it necessary to abolish this contract, it may announce its invalidity, but the execution period must be implemented six months after the announcement]. Then, it will handle it itself. However, this move is only out of extreme necessity. If Soviet Russia does not push too hard, it will never take this action. Li Shaogeng, the acting Chinese Director-General of the Railway, is particularly unwilling to stir up unexpected waves with this, so he has been doing his best to mediate as a third party to bring the opinions of both sides closer and solve the problem in an orderly manner through the conference. It is also heard that the Chinese committee members have also drafted the telephone part of the proposal and will submit it for approval when the exchange of views is smooth this time.

Wuhu Express News 11

The military and police authorities here, in order to consolidate local public security, have implemented a temporary curfew starting last night. After 12 o'clock, traffic is cut off. Soldiers are stationed in the suburbs and at major roads. It is heard that the curfew will last until the end of this month.

The Anhui Provincial Chamber of Commerce held its second representative assembly on the 5th of this month. Due to disputes over reorganization, the matter remained unresolved. Representatives were dispatched to Beijing and the provincial capital to petition the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and the Provincial Party Headquarters. The representatives returned to Wuhu one after another yesterday. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce believes that the second representative assembly of the association should be held as usual, but made no statement on the reorganization issue. The association reopened the assembly this afternoon, concluded the proposals of the second session, and then adjourned. The reorganization issue has to be postponed. Four members of the provincial government committee, Ma Jidi, Jin Weixi, Li Yinsheng, and Zhang Keyao, recently sent a telegram to the Hefei natives association in Wuhu, stating that Hefei levied a special land tax for disaster relief regardless of the suffering of the people. They expressed extreme hatred and ordered the county magistrates to be dismissed and punished if they obeyed Yuan Lichen and dared to collect the tax. They have also telegraphed the central government to strongly advocate on behalf of the people.

Ma Fuxiang, Chairman of the Provincial Government, Wang Zhijue, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, and Ma Jidi, Director of the He'an Office, jointly issued an order to the counties, stating that in these difficult times, the local area is unstable and the national army has other tasks. In order to be able to take both into account, if bandits occur in various counties in the future, the county magistrates should lead the local militia and police to suppress them. Those who rashly request troops and exaggerate the situation will be severely punished.

The Anhui Provincial Department of Education has scheduled the second provincial education administrative conference to be held on July 1st. Ma Jingwen, Director of the Wuhu County Education Bureau, has prepared proposals on education administration funds, school education, and compulsory education, and is scheduled to go to the provincial capital on the 28th to attend. (23rd) Local correspondence

Songjiang

The provincial government ordered the arrest of the lake bandit leader and his gang leader, Taibao A Xu. They have been harassing merchants on Taihu Lake. After being severely suppressed by the military and police, they fled back to Liu Siqiao, Jinshan County, where they gather and disperse unpredictably. The Jinshan County magistrate had previously telegraphed the provincial government, which forwarded the information to the three-province bandit suppression commander for suppression to eliminate the root cause. Now, the provincial government has issued a general order to all its agencies to offer a reward of one thousand yuan for the arrest. The county government convened a meeting of district chiefs. The county government has many cases awaiting handling by various districts. It is now scheduled to convene a meeting of district chiefs on the 28th of this month to discuss and issue administrative expenses notices to various districts for compliance.

A tenant accused the landlord of theft. Li Zhou, a resident of the west of the city, rented out her surplus house to Lei Jiajun after her husband died. Recently, the Lei family suddenly accused the landlord of theft. Yesterday, the county government opened a court hearing. According to Li Zhou, Lei borrowed 350 yuan from her twice but refused to issue an IOU. Because he pried open the door twice attempting rape, she was forced to lend him the money to avoid losing her chastity. It was unbearable to live with him, so she moved elsewhere to avoid trouble. The items she moved that day were all her own. Moreover, Lei's servant, Xu Siwu, saw that the accusations were all slander. After questioning the witness Xu Siwu, the case was judged to require further investigation. Li Zhou was ordered to post bail pending interrogation.

Bandit robbery near Wuku. In the south of Wuku, Yuanmao and Shenjiabang were robbed on two successive nights. Bandits attempted to rob a certain family in Yuanmao. They had already pried open the door when the head of the household saw the light and quickly fled to a neighboring village to call for help, sounding the gong. The bandits then scattered and fled. It is heard that four families in Shenjiabang were robbed, but the extent of the losses is unknown.

Suzhou

County police team's anti-bandit measures. Due to the resurgence of banditry in various villages, the county police brigade planned preventive measures yesterday (25th). It was decided that the first squadron would be stationed in Weiting, Xiangcheng, and Taiping Bridge to defend against the Yangcheng area. The second squadron would be stationed in Xietang, Chefang, and Chenmu to defend against the Chenghu area. The third squadron would be stationed in Guangfu, Puzhuang, and Xuzhuang to defend against the Taihu area. The fourth squadron will be responsible for garrisoning the urban area. The Department of Finance dispatches personnel to raise funds. Due to the urgent need for funds, the Department of Finance has specially dispatched a committee member to Suzhou to raise 20,000 yuan from the Finance Bureau. Zhu Boying, the head of the levy section, borrowed 10,000 yuan from various businesses and guilds. Interest will accrue from July 1st at a rate of 1.2% per month, to be repaid from this year's busy season tax revenue.

Military and police organize an inspection office. The local authorities received a telegram from the Songhu Garrison Headquarters to organize a military and police inspection office. It is scheduled to be established today (26th) and will inspect newspapers.

After Chen Yi and others were decided to be transferred to the Army Prison. The third sub-prison on Siqian Street will transfer prisoners awaiting trial, Chen Yi and thirty others, to the Army Second Prison. This matter has attracted the attention of the legal community in Suzhou and Shanghai. It is now learned that this matter occurred because of prison riots in the sub-prison. The Ministry of Justice secretly ordered the High Court to handle the matter and dispatched Wang Yuanhuan, the section chief of the Prison Department, to Suzhou to meet with the President of the High Court, Lin, the Chief Prosecutor, Wang, the Clerk, Wei, and the Deputy Warden to decide to transfer Chen and others.

Men resembling wounded soldiers forcibly pawn old goods. Yesterday (25th) at around 8:00 AM, men resembling wounded soldiers carried cotton quilts to the Fu Yuan pawnshop in Huqiu and Bantang and forcibly pawned them. More and more people gathered, and the pawnshop could not refuse. They closed the door tightly and telegraphed the County Public Security Bureau for instructions on how to maintain commercial influence. The director of the bureau, after receiving the report, had no suitable solution to stop them. Therefore, he convened various agencies at the Railway Hotel outside the city at 6:00 PM to discuss a plan. The results of the discussion are unknown due to time constraints. Whether the pawnshop will open for business today depends on whether a suitable solution can be found.

Bandit robbery and murder at Taiping Bridge. At around 2:00 AM on the morning of the 24th, bandits from Jiangbei broke into the house of Dai Yongxing, a farmer in Wangjiabang, Taiping Bridge, Xiangcheng Township. Armed with sharp weapons, they robbed rice and wheat. Dai Yongxing's wife, Wu, was awakened from her sleep and tried to chop at the bandits with an axe. Unexpectedly, she was wounded in the head by the bandits. The bandits then carried the loot and fled. Dai chased them outside the door, where he was tied up by the bandits and beaten to death with wooden sticks. The local police station heard about the incident and pursued the bandits, but to no avail. They reported to the county yesterday for instructions.

Wuxi

The third batch of wounded soldiers arrive in Wuxi. Two batches of wounded soldiers, totaling 95, have arrived earlier. Yesterday, at around 12:00 AM, another third batch of 64 wounded soldiers arrived. This morning (25th) at 8:00 AM, another 15 wounded soldiers arrived. The Wuxi Committee for Comforting Wounded Soldiers sent personnel to the station to receive them and hired three boats to transport the wounded soldiers to the No. 22 Rear Hospital in Huishan Town for treatment.

A drama troupe causes trouble and is ordered to stop performing. There are four theaters in Wuxi, including Qing Sheng, Xin Zhongyang, Xin Xin, and Di Yi Tai Zhong Sheng. The Xin Zhongyang Theater is the most prosperous and profitable. The others are not doing well and have been repeatedly closed and reopened. Because of the theaters, accidents have occurred repeatedly. Previously, Xin Zhongyang had a conflict with the audience, resulting in a bloody tragedy. Both parties filed lawsuits, and the county government almost split. After mediation, the lawsuits were dropped. The night before last, Qing Sheng Theater outside Guangfu Gate reported that Inspector Cha Rongqiu (an employee of the Jinghu Railway) had a fight with Liu Hanchao, a waiting officer of the Public Security Bureau. They were taken to the second branch of the Public Security Bureau and transferred to the County Public Security Bureau, which transferred them to the County Government. Yesterday, Officer Yu Chengxiang opened a court hearing. As a result of the interrogation, Liu Hanchao was ordered to return. Cha Rongqiu was sent to the Wuxi Station master for investigation. Liu Hanchao went to the Labor Hospital for treatment and asked someone to petition the County Government for compensation for the damage. County Magistrate Sun Zuji believed that the theater had repeatedly caused incidents, and at this time of unrest, trouble was foreseeable. Yesterday, he specially instructed the Chief of Political Police, Wu Zhengrong, to order the theater to suspend performances from today. Chief Wu followed the order immediately.

All silk factory workers petition. The labor and management of Wuxi silk industry re-negotiated the labor-management contract and formally signed it the day before yesterday. Unexpectedly, the management suddenly regretted the agreement and firmly refused to sign it, causing the labor-management dispute that was about to be resolved to break down. It is learned that yesterday afternoon, the labor representatives (Silk Factory Workers' Union) specially convened the 19th joint meeting of workers' representatives from various factories. The number of attendees was unusually large. After discussion, two methods were decided: (A) To petition the Party and government organs to resolve the issue fairly, and the workers' representatives from various factories will immediately petition the County Party Headquarters and the County Government. Since the management has reneged on the already resolved solution, the labor will not stop until the goal of implementing the entire draft is achieved. (B) Female workers' representatives from various factories will do their best to dissuade female members to prevent any overstepping of boundaries. After the meeting, they will separately petition the County Party Headquarters and the County Government to request relief, and all workers will go to the County Party Headquarters to petition. Zhang Ren, the executive of the Civil Training Committee, and Ji Jun, the Minister of the Organization Department, received them and promised to resolve the issue reasonably. Then, all the workers went to the County Government to petition. County Magistrate Gu Shi was out on official business, so the second section chief, Lu Qi, received them on his behalf and promised to send personnel to investigate and convene the transforming party to hold a meeting to mediate the conditions already agreed upon by the labor and management, which will definitely be realized and will not disappoint the labor. The workers were satisfied and dispersed.

Changzhou

The patrol team leader dies from serious injuries. Liu Lin, the patrol team leader (i.e., the security regiment) of the Shangtuan branch in Xin'an Town, the fifth district of Wu County, was killed by Xu Fuchun, a soldier who had been dismissed from the team, out of revenge. Another soldier, Wang Yunlong, went to rescue him and was also stabbed. He was sent to Wujin Hospital for treatment. It is learned that patrol team leader Liu Lin died of his injuries at 11:50 PM on the 23rd. On the 24th, Qian Yuzhen, the head of the Shangtuan Headquarters, and Zhang Gongwang, the head of the fifth district, separately sent letters to the County Court and the County Government to report the case. Yang Kong, the chief prosecutor of the County Court, led officials to the scene at 5:00 PM to inspect the body. The examination revealed 18 or 19 knife wounds on the body, the most serious of which was in the abdomen. The stabbed soldier, Wang Yunlong, was also examined and found to have five or six stab wounds. The prosecutor briefly questioned the family of the deceased and then prepared a coffin for burial. The murderer, Xu Fuchun, is still being actively pursued.

A boat on its way to Jiting Bridge is robbed. A boat sailing from Wu County to Jiting Bridge was robbed at about 1:00 AM on the 24th while passing through the Shiwudong Bridge area in Yan Township. The boatmen were tied up and beaten, and the boat was searched for about an hour before the robbers left. It is estimated that they stole over two hundred yuan in cash and three gold rings. Fortunately, hundreds of yuan in paper money were not stolen.

Finance Department committee member goes from Changzhou to Wuxi. Zhuang Yeguang, a committee member of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, was ordered to come to Changzhou to guard and collect 20,000 yuan in allotted silver. On the 24th, he contacted County Magistrate Wu and Liu Hongzhao, the director of the Finance Bureau, regarding everything. Director Liu promised to find a way to raise the money. Committee member Zhuang had to go to Wuxi and Yixing counties to guard and collect allotted funds, so he immediately took a car to Wuxi.

Jiangyin

Water police seize a large amount of opium. Yu Chaoting, the supervising officer of the 20th detachment of the Water Public Security Team, seized a large amount of opium, totaling 55 large packages weighing several thousand taels, near Huangshan Port on the 23rd. Captain He telegraphed Jiang Chao, the district chief of Zhenjiang, to send the Daya warship to Cheng to pick it up within days.

Due to local economic difficulties, the director resigns. Cheng County is busy with tax collection, but due to the poor harvest this year, tax revenue has decreased. Since the reform, the number of local organs has increased significantly. For example, the monthly police expenses have increased from 1,050 yuan to over 5,000 yuan. The Funds Production Office cannot raise funds. Since March and April, arrears have accumulated. From last year to now, it owes more than 100,000 yuan to various money houses. The debt is high and there is no more borrowing. The current director and deputy director of the Funds Production Office, Xia Sunhu and Zhu Fei, cannot cope and have firmly resigned to the County Government.

Panic over skyrocketing rice prices. Since the fall of silver prices, the prices of all goods have soared, and rice prices have also skyrocketed. In recent days, it has reached 20 yuan. On the 23rd, it was sold for 19.2 yuan, and unofficially at 20 yuan. The public is in a state of panic. Because rice merchants have no goods arriving, they restrict rice buyers to only a few dou. Under these circumstances, the livelihood of the common people is truly unbearable. The Warehouse Committee has put forward seven opinions to County Magistrate Li, as follows: (1) The Funds Production Office should automatically offer to pledge and deposit grain funds in various estates and Changhua, and all should be transferred. (2) The grain funds are only over 20,000 yuan. If they are distributed to various villages for price stabilization, it will not help. Efforts should be made to raise large amounts of funds for simultaneous distribution. (3) In recent years, the Funds Production Office has used the custody of grain funds to divert funds for party affairs and various local expenses, amounting to tens of thousands. All should be ordered to return the funds. (4) Impartial personnel should be recommended to persuade local and overseas merchants to donate funds. (5) Has the funds accumulated before 1922 been distributed to various villages to stabilize prices or distributed to poor households, and have records been reported and announced? Please send personnel to investigate. (6) Whether the price stabilization should be organized by the entire county or distributed to various villages and districts for separate fund-raising, a sound method should be studied and implemented. (7) The Grain Funds used by the former Military and Police Joint Defense Office and the Public Security Team established during the Qing Township period, amounting to tens of thousands, should be returned to the Grain Funds Office. Measures to deal with local prostitutes. Because there are many local prostitutes in the county, the county government will discuss emergency measures for dealing with arrested local prostitutes at the three-day county government meeting. It was resolved that after the first arrest, the Public Security Bureau will take photos and display them to the public, and order a guarantor to hand them over to their families for custody. The second time, they will be expelled from the county along with their families and sent to the local rehabilitation center for custody after it is established. Provincial Party Headquarters investigates the accusation. Gao Kangfu, a member of the organizing committee of the County Party Headquarters, was accused by Party member Zhu and others to the Provincial Party Headquarters, which sent Wang Zhichao on the 23rd to Cheng to investigate.

Zhenjiang

Jiangsu Products Exhibition Hall to open soon. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mining previously ordered all counties to select and manufacture the latest products or draw and frame the research results and send them to the department for review and exhibition before the opening of the Agricultural and Mining Products Exhibition Hall. Now, the factory believes that the deadline is approaching, but not many factories have complied. In addition to sending personnel to work with Qi Lunji and Hou Zhenfeng, the directors of the exhibition hall, to sort out all the agricultural and mining products that have been sent, and ordering the Forestry Bureau to send personnel to assist in sorting out the forestry products, it also issued an order yesterday urging all counties to quickly comply with the previous order to select and manufacture various specimens and send them to the province for review and exhibition in order to open as soon as possible.

Yangzhou

Telegraphs to request exemption from sending wounded soldiers to Yangzhou. The County Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force Wounded Soldiers Rear Management Committee on the 23rd, stating that since the military uprising in 1927, Jiangdu has been a key point in northern Jiangsu, so that the rebel army's southward invasion and the national army's northward expedition have all regarded it as a necessary route. In total, there have been more than ten times of military disasters, resulting in losses of hundreds of thousands of yuan. The local vitality has been greatly damaged, and business has been depressed. So far, the debt is so large that it cannot be compensated. In addition, in the past two years, banditry has been rampant and disasters have been frequent, and the people are in dire straits. In June of this year, the Jiangdu County Government was approved to forward the telegram from the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs ordering them to seek places to accommodate wounded soldiers. The county government telegraphed back based on the meeting situation on file. Yesterday, the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs continued to reply, stating that if wounded soldiers arrive, it is hoped that they will strive to prepare for supplies and treatment. The county government forwarded the information again. It is reported that the local Jiang area is in distress as described above. If wounded soldiers are sent to Yangzhou again, ordering them to prepare supplies and treatment is actually a painful situation where they cannot win. Please consider and approve the request to exempt sending wounded soldiers to Yangzhou. We are extremely grateful.

Guerrilla Headquarters to be established in Northern Jiangsu. Liu Zuhan, the guerrilla commander of Northern Jiangsu, dispatched his staff officer, Hua Jun, and adjutant, Shen Song, to Yangzhou to select a location for the headquarters. Hua and others went to the Chamber of Commerce on the 23rd to state their intentions, saying that they had found a suitable house in the back of He Garden and were arranging it. Once they reported back, they would work with Liu in Yangzhou.

Boatmen come to the city to complain. The boatmen in Sanyi River were found to have wheat by Xia, the police captain stationed there. Six boatmen, including Yu Da, Ni, and Liu Yutai, were detained and taken to the city. Yesterday, the police brigade transferred them to the court. This morning (24th), more than a dozen family members of the boatmen came to the city and went to the County Government Police Team and the County Court to complain, claiming that Captain Xia had arbitrarily arrested the common people and used torture to extract confessions, requesting justice. It is still unknown how it will be resolved.

Jingjiang

The Security Regiment intercepts a bandit ship. The Security Regiment of the Eighth District received a tip on the morning of the 21st that a bandit ship was moored in Dajue Port, about three miles away from Sidunzi. There were more than 40 bandits on board with box guns. Regiment Commander Li led his team to suppress the bandits. The bandits heard the news and fled across the river. One sea ship was still moored there, with many stolen goods on board. According to Guanglin, a Xiaohua officer, who reported that he was robbed by bandits the day before, losing about 2,000 yuan in silver, clothes, and jewelry. The bandits also left behind a Lafu gun. Regiment Commander Li reported that all the thieves on the ship were possessions and immediately opened the ship to Sidunzi to await the County Government's disposal.

Another kidnapping and killing case in Eastern Township. Song Xiaotong, who lived in Longwenqiaodai, about five li away from Tuqiao, was quite wealthy. At 11:00 PM on the 20th, more than a dozen bandits suddenly broke into the door. The family heard the noise and fled, but his old mother was too slow to escape and was brutally killed by the bandits. Also, a young girl, the sister of the wife, was kidnapped by the bandits. Before leaving, the bandits fired guns to show off.

The army arrests a large number of suspected criminals. Yin Tianmin, the captain of the First Guerrilla Team, and Wang Huaiyin, the captain of the Second Police Team, arrested a large number of bandits in Jijiashi, Ningjieshi, Shaojiadai, Guanglingzhen, and other places, including Yuan Qiansan, Yuan Changhua, Xu Lin'er, Pan Linguan, Xiong Bosheng, Xiong Jinzhao, Gu Qixiang, Ding Deming, Gu Lansheng, Zhu Peicheng, and more than 30 others. After interrogation by the trial officer Yin Cheng, it was found that most of them were good people and more than a dozen were released immediately. The rest were temporarily detained and could be released if there was reliable guarantee.

Gaoyou

Hall order to restore business in Xingye. All shops in the county have suspended business since 1927 due to military influence. The Civil Hall has now issued a special order to the County Government, stating that the county has suffered a poor harvest and the poor have no access to loans, making life difficult. Remedial measures must be taken. The local pawn industry should be ordered to continue operating as appropriate to provide some relief. All loans that have expired or have not expired should be extended for three months, and interest should be calculated according to the regulations. County Magistrate Wang has ordered all pawnshops to comply. The young nephew of Wang is kidnapped. The young nephew of Wang Chunbo, a farmer in Weiwangzhuang, has been kidnapped by bandits since last winter and there has been no news of him. Wang learned of his whereabouts the day before yesterday and heard that he had been contacted by a certain village official and would be redeemed for 1,500 yuan.

The District Chief is accused and thoroughly investigated. Zhang Shiyan, the District Chief of the Second District of Gaoyou, has been accused by Zhou and other citizens of the district in the Civil Hall of prostituting, gambling, and abusing his power. County Magistrate Wang received an order from the Hall yesterday and commissioned Guo Shixi, the District Chief of the First District, and Wan Diankui, the District Chief of the Fifth District, to conduct a thorough investigation.

Accounting Director transferred to Bureau Chief. Zhou Sixai, the accounting director of the Gaoyou Finance Bureau, has been appointed by the Finance Hall as the director of the Jingjiang County Finance Bureau. It is heard that Zhou has left for his new post this morning (21st).

Jiashan

Bandits rob rice in Gan Kiln. Rice prices have been rising day by day, with Dongshuang costing 18.4 yuan per dan. Those who seek a living feel it is difficult to eat. Last night, dozens of poor people and bandits came to Qianjiabang, Gan Kiln, and robbed rice from house to house. Even those with three or five liters of rice for the next day were not spared. The public is extremely panicked. If rice prices are not suppressed, the robbery may be difficult to stop. Two cases of kidnapping and robbery in Hongyang Port. Yesterday, four bandit ships and 40 bandits from the northeast of Jiashan Dingzha came to Hongyang Port. After landing, they rushed to the home of farmer Gu Sanqing and demanded 1,000 yuan in silver, but they were unsuccessful. They ransacked the boxes and cabinets at will, losing nearly 100 yuan. Seeing that there was nothing else of value, they kidnapped Gu's younger brother, Long Shengzi Amaotou, and threatened to redeem him for 2,000 yuan. Then they went to the house of Hu Atao in Waihan, robbed it clean, shot three workers, and lost about 400 yuan and more than 60 shi of white rice. After the robbery, they left.

Nantong

Anti-bandit measures on the coast of Nantong. Recently, sea bandits have frequently invaded the coastal areas of Nantong, forcing fishermen to pay protection money and hijacking merchant ships. Residents of Luken, Pengjiao, and other areas have all organized fishermen's groups to cooperate with the garrison troops to defend the coast. Blockhouses are built at strategic locations and military telephones are installed. The Fan Gong Dike is being rebuilt into a motor road, and construction will begin in the autumn. The Security Regiment temporarily uses a recruitment system. The Nantong County Government believes that the organization of the Security Regiment should legally convene district residents to serve as soldiers. However, the banditry in the four villages is very strong and it is difficult to carry out. County Magistrate Zhang has specially approved the province to organize and establish Security Regiments in all districts. Temporary recruitment of temporary soldiers will be allowed. It will be renamed the Temporary Security Regiment. Once the banditry is quelled, the Security District Regiment will be reorganized in accordance with regulations.

Survey of the tidal disasters along the Yangtze River. The Nantong Yao and Wang ports have been hit by tidal disasters. In recent days, the farmland of Zhang Zongwei and Bai Jiawei has been collapsing rapidly. The collapse of Langshan is imminent. On the 24th, County Magistrate Zhang, Director Yao of the Construction Bureau, and representatives from all walks of life went to the disaster area to investigate. In addition to telegraphing the province for relief, they are rushing to allocate funds for rescue work.

The Liu Changyan case. It has recently been heard that Liu Changyan, the former County Magistrate of the county, has been repeatedly accused. The Provincial Government has decided to send the various cases of Liu Changyan's illegality to the court for trial. Pinghu

Lu Lansheng's house was robbed. The house of Lu Lansheng, a carpenter in Xiaoniangbang, Northwest Village, Jiudai, Xindai, was suddenly attacked by bandits at late night on the 23rd. More than a dozen bandits with thread guns and machetes broke into the door and pointed at the owner, forcing him to show them where the silver was hidden, injuring the owner with knives and robbing him of 100 yuan and cloth clothes. The next day, the owner reported to the Public Security Bureau and requested an arrest.

A monk drowned while bathing. Three monks in Baoben Temple bathed in the river in front of the temple yesterday, the 24th, because it was hot. When they went ashore, one monk was missing. Because the river was quite deep and the monk could not swim, he drowned.

The Provincial Department of Agriculture and Forestry begins preparations. Investigate the amount of cash and silver. Arrested key criminals involved in counterfeiting national currency.
