He sent them to the court for punishment according to law.

Xiaoshan

Robbery on the road in broad daylight. A local villager surnamed Zheng, who was selling fruits such as peaches and plums near Suoqian Town, was robbed by four bandits while walking to Xihuitou Chi Tou Shen. They robbed him of 19 yuan and 27 jiao in cash and pushed Zheng into the mud.

The County Government conducts a census in Jin County. The townships and towns of Xiaoshan have already established and organized the County Government to conduct a census of the entire county. Yesterday, a special order was issued to each district office to submit a census table of the population in the district to the county for review and compilation of the county census table.

The amount of bayberry shipped out. Bayberry is a specialty of Xiaoshan. This year, the fruit production is unusually abundant. Since it was launched on the market on the 13th of this month, more than 45,000 units have been shipped out by railway, worth about 500,000 yuan. There are still three or four tenths of the fruit waiting to be transported from various mountains. This is also good news for agricultural production.

Xiaoshan

The Sanjiangkou robbery and injury case. There are usually three or four small grocery stores near Sanjiangkou, opposite Linpu. At about 10:00 PM on the 19th, six or seven bandits with foreign accents suddenly came to the Chengda Grocery Store, broke in through the screen door, and robbed them openly with torches and clubs. The hostess, Tian Shen, was awakened from her dream and shouted for help, causing her to be injured in the leg by the bandits. Fortunately, it was not fatal. Later, merchant ships from Hangzhou and Zhuji arrived, and the bandits fled. After checking, it was found that they had been robbed of more than 100 yuan in silver and clothes.

Illegal village and town chiefs are accused. Since the establishment of village and town councils in Xiaoshan, most of the village and town chiefs have been upright in their conduct, but there are also many who act arbitrarily and extort money. For example, Xu Bingkui, the chief of Xuanheng Village, used the stamp to extort three yuan in silver, and Xu Yisheng, the chief of Wu Tu Village, privately charged two jiao per mu for reporting fees, and also forbade the management and purchase of ponds and marshes. As a result, the people were resentful, and it is no wonder that people often sue the county and the province.

Shangyu

The entanglement over the suspension of Chunhui School. The school board of Chunhui Middle School suspended the school due to the kidnapping case, causing more than 400 students to be at a loss. The people of the county did not approve of this, believing that the kidnapping case and the school were two separate matters. It is necessary to rescue the principals who were kidnapped, but the school cannot be suspended because of the kidnapping case with the eight characters "protecting no one and unable to defend themselves." Moreover, the school receives a subsidy of 2,000 yuan from the province every year, so it is not appropriate to suspend classes and allow the students to waste their studies. Moreover, the school was funded by the late school president Chen 　　Lan and Chen Ziqiu Shan, founded by Jing Hengyi, and Fan Shoukang has been in charge for ten years. Recently, the library has been enriched, the sports field has been built, and the new school buildings have been expanded with a new atmosphere. Its perfect equipment is the crown of the current private middle schools. After this incident, the school authorities only made one meeting to suspend classes, and no one was responsible for the end of the school year and the relief of students who lost their school, which is very regrettable. It is also known that Chunzhong students established the School Protection Movement Committee on the 19th. Regarding the fact that the bandits can come and go freely in the areas where the military and police are stationed and wander during the day and kidnap and cause bloodshed at night, it is due to the dereliction of duty of the military and police and for the sake of their own future, they cannot sit idly by and issue a statement to schools, institutions, and organizations across the country requesting sympathy and assistance.

Shi Huaimao is sentenced to death again. Shi Huaimao of Nijiapu was sentenced to two death sentences and two prison terms totaling 15 years and 4 months, and deprived of his civil rights for life by the county's retrial on December 30 of the same year for the case of adultery, injury, and poisoning Zhang Depei and his wife, and poisoning Zhang Guixian unsuccessfully in October 1928. Shi refused to accept the appeal and appealed to the Supreme Court, which revoked the original judgment and remanded it to the High Court for retrial. Earlier this month, the High Court retried and sentenced Shi Huaimao to death again. It is heard that he will be sent back to his place of origin for execution in the coming days.

Jiangshan

Jiangshan County is strictly guarding against bandits and communists. Jiangshan is an important place in eastern Zhejiang and the throat of Fujian entering Zhejiang. The defense is extremely important. Recently, the Guangfeng County Police Team in Jiangxi Province colluded with bandits and communists to occupy the county seat in the cold night, killing officials and releasing prisoners. The momentum was huge. Guangcheng is only 50 miles away from Jiangshan. It is now heard that the bandits have gathered in the 42nd capital, which is even closer, and there is a sense of imminent danger. Because of the emergency, County Magistrate Mi repeatedly telegraphed the province to send elite troops to suppress them, and personally supervised the military and police day and night to strictly guard and check travelers and hotels to prevent bandit spies from infiltrating. He also sent a team to the border to strengthen the defense. Also, because the county had previously uncovered the case of Guan Zengshou, who smuggled guns, and Guan was a member of the Guangfeng Police Team, which was obviously related to this rebellion, it is heard that he has sent cadres overnight to send the prisoners to Jinhua to avoid negligence. However, the garrison troops are limited. It is deeply hoped that the province will transfer heavy troops to strengthen the defense as soon as possible to avoid tragedy.

Letters received

Liaoning Official Mines Decide to Seek Merchants for Exploitation 12

Shenyang Correspondence: The mining areas in Liaoning Province are abundant, several times that of the entire country. The former Industry Department presented to the former Provincial Governor's Office to retain over 160 locations for official operation, but they have not been developed. It is a great pity to waste these resources. Now, the Department of Agriculture and Mines has carefully planned and decided to tender for the exploitation of the remaining 160+ mining areas, except for a few that will be operated by the government itself, in order to develop the resources. Eleven articles of provisional regulations for opening official mines and unexploited mines, ten articles of inspection rules, and fourteen articles of simplified regulations for collecting proceeds from mineral sales have been formulated. These have been submitted to the Provincial Government Committee for approval and will be promulgated and implemented by the Department. The following is a transcript of the opening regulations: (Article 1) All official and unexploited mines in the province, except for those that are selectively retained (the number of retained mines will be determined by the Department), will be tendered for exploitation. The exploitation methods will be handled in accordance with these regulations, unless otherwise stipulated by law. (Article 2) When merchants apply for these mining areas, they must still comply with the procedures outlined in the Mining Law. However, the area of application must be surveyed by a special commissioner sent by the Department, who will provide a map and explanation. The merchant must submit five copies of the map for separate filing. (Article 3) The amount of capital required for exploitation will be determined by the Department based on the size of the planned mine and the number of acres. The funds must be deposited in cash in a reliable bank or merchant house. A receipt will be issued first, and the funds can only be withdrawn when the mining license is issued, in order to prevent delays in exploitation. The number of capital to be prepared by ordinary mine merchants, which was previously approved by the Department for revision, does not apply to these regulations. (Article 4) Merchants applying to exploit official mines will have a preparation period of three months from the date of issuance of the mining license and an implementation period of six months for exploitation. If the deadline is exceeded, the mining rights will be revoked. If there are special circumstances requiring an extension, it must not exceed the provisions of Article 46 of the Mining Law (failure to start work after registration or suspension of work for more than one year). (Article 5) During the preparation period, an office must be established within the first month or a company must be organized in accordance with the Company Law. (Article 6) In order to supervise and guide the implementation of mining plans and the progress of affairs, the Department may assign an inspector to each mining area based on its size. The miner is responsible for the monthly salary, but the amount will be determined by the Department separately. The aforementioned inspector will be dispatched when the mine is being prepared, and the rules of operation will be determined by the Department separately. (Article 7) For each mine extracted from an officially reserved mine, the merchant is to calculate, at the end of each month, the total proceeds sold at market price. The Department will collect 2% to 4% as appropriate. The aforementioned collection method and amount may be determined by the Department on an ad hoc basis. (Article 8) Merchants who apply to mine officially reserved mines are allowed to present the amount of ore extracted, or the amount tested, if there is no exploitative value. The Department may waive or audit the seventh regulation to see if it applies. (Article 9) The term for applying to open mines officially reserved with gold, silver, copper, iron, tin, lead, and coal is from 25 to 35 years. For clay, talc, gypsum, and zinc, the term is from 20 to 30 years. After the term expires, the miner is allowed to continue mining. However, if the miner has special circumstances and cannot continue mining, and the Department recruits a third party to mine, the real estate and buildings in the mining area must be received by the Department and paid with a corresponding value of gold. The provisions of the preceding article do not apply to those who suspend work midway. (Article 10) If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, the Department of Agriculture and Mines may amend them at any time and submit them to the Provincial Government for record. (Article 11) These regulations shall come into effect from the date of deliberation and promulgation by the Provincial Government Committee.

Liaoning Province Plans to Establish a Match Monopoly Bureau 13

Shenyang Correspondence: Zhang Zhenyi, Director of the Department of Finance, believes that matches are a daily necessity. The match merchants in the province are only Guandong, Huilin, Sanming, and Sheng Sheng, four companies whose business is relatively developed and sales are quite extensive. However, recently there have been unscrupulous merchants counterfeiting brands and selling at inconsistent prices, which has greatly affected the match industry. Moreover, domestic matches have been under pressure from Swedish matches for years and have been unable to resist. In order to develop national interests and revitalize Dong Province's industry, the Department plans to establish a Match Monopoly Bureau to purchase and sell all domestic matches through the Bureau. Merchants are not allowed to set up factories for manufacturing without permission. Imports are also purchased by the Bureau in order to protect profits. The organizational charter of the Match Monopoly Bureau has been drafted and submitted to the Northeast Political Affairs Committee. It will be formally established once approved. (18th)

The Perilous State of Industry and Commerce in Jilin 14

Appeal to the Provincial Government for Relief

Jilin Correspondence: The industry and commerce in the provincial capital are under the pressure of gold notes and are struggling to survive. In total, the member firms of the two industry and commerce associations owe Japanese-owned Manchuria Bank and Jilin Bank no less than 600,000 yuan in gold notes. Compared to the past, it has risen by more than one time, causing even greater damage. Not only is the market bleak, but there is also a complete stagnation. Previously, the leaders of each industry appealed to the two commerce and industry associations to plead with the provincial government to order the banks in the provincial capital to provide sufficient loans to alleviate the immediate crisis. The provincial government believes that whether the banks can provide loans as much as possible is another issue, and the standards and limits for loans requested by the industry and commerce sectors, as well as all methods of mortgage guarantees, must be thoroughly examined and pre-defined. Therefore, the government ordered the two associations to draft six articles of measures: (1) In order to avoid the soaring of Japanese gold, causing disaster. All industry and commerce firms in the provincial capital with lending relationships with foreign banks, or those without foreign lending but with legitimate needs, should request domestic banks to provide sufficient loans for relief. (2) The form of industry and commerce firm lending has always been divided into two types: mortgage loans and credit loans. For this request for relief, what kind of procedures are appropriate for the industry and commerce firms receiving loans? It is proposed that the lending banks and the borrowing industry and commerce firms negotiate on their own. (3) Whether the pledges or credit guarantees prepared by the borrowing industry and commerce firms are accurate should be thoroughly investigated by the lending banks. If necessary, the industry and commerce associations will assist in the handling. (4) The interest rate on foreign bank loans ranges from a minimum of 8% to a maximum of 1% and 1.4%. This request for relief also asks that the interest rates set by the banks be specially reduced with reference to this interest rate. (5) The lending of funds by the banks is often difficult for the borrower to repay on time due to the short term. This request for relief is to maintain the market, resist foreign economic invasion, and save interests. It is proposed that the banks extend the term exceptionally to serve as an example. (6) The above measures are based on the lending rules of the banks, each with its own regulations. However, due to repeated provincial orders, they have been jointly reviewed to determine whether they are appropriate. The provincial government believes that the current rise in gold notes and the panic in the market must be maintained by some means. However, the lending of funds by the banks, although no more than two types of mortgages and credit, must have a certain and unchangeable process. The two layers of requested reduction of interest rates and extension of terms, whether they can be done, are still to be negotiated. The actual number of industry and commerce sectors in the provincial capital that are currently under the pressure of gold notes, and whether they can be rescued based on their recent business conditions, and how to classify and determine the loan amount, must also be carefully considered. The government ordered the competent Department of Agriculture and Mines to investigate and invite the banks to discuss and reply. The Department also found it difficult and first invited the two industry and commerce associations to negotiate. Yan Aichen, Vice President of the Chamber of Commerce, and Hu Weiqing, President of the Industrial Association, both arrived at the Department for discussion. Subsequently, it was agreed that the first step would be for the two associations to investigate the number of industry and commerce firms that need loans and negotiate the loan procedures with the banking group. After the loan procedures are ready, the second step will be for the Department to convene a joint meeting of all relevant parties to decide on measures to be submitted to the province for implementation. The two associations are currently starting the investigation.

The Suspension of the Jiangsu Province Cooperation Training Institute 15

The provincial treasury can eliminate burdens.

The cause will not be interrupted.

In order to promote cooperation and improve the economy of farmers, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mines established the Cooperative Instructor Training Institute in the 17th year, and in the 18th year, it established eight provincial instructor offices in various counties, and continued to run the second phase of the Cooperative Instructor Training Institute. It was planning to expand the plan and proceed by region, but due to the provincial treasury deficit, it had to tighten up, and the original instructor offices established with provincial funds had to be cut down to save money. However, at a time when the central government is actively promoting cooperation, it seems difficult to stop the cooperative cause that has already been established in Jiangsu Province halfway. Therefore, the Department of Agriculture has formulated an economic measure, that is, to reassign the graduates of the first and second phases to work in various counties under the command and supervision of the county government. All counties that have already approved the collection of two-point agricultural improvement mu donations will pay the cooperative expenses and the salaries of the instructors from special funds. The treatment of the instructors is the same as that of the section members of the county government, and the Department has submitted a special case to the provincial government meeting for approval and implementation on the 24th of this month.

Shanghai-Hangzhou-Mogan Joint Transportation is Implemented 16

The Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau has designated Mogan Mountain as a summer resort. As the hot summer season approaches, the number of Chinese and foreign tourists visiting for summer vacation or sightseeing will inevitably increase. In order to facilitate tourists, it has negotiated joint transportation with the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Bureau. It is now ready, but the formal contract must be signed in early July. Before the formal signing, both parties have drafted six temporary measures for joint transportation, which will be implemented from July 1st. The Highway Bureau will set up a joint transportation office at No. 368 on Mogan Mountain, and offices will be set up at the Chengzhan and Gengcun stations to handle joint transportation matters. Many new-style buses have been purchased. The bus will depart from Chengzhan station at 2:15 pm every day (connecting the bus departing from Shanghai North Station at 9:00 am) and will arrive at the mountain at about 5:30 pm. In addition, many small chartered cars are available at Gengcun in Hangzhou. Sedan chairs are available at the Gengcun office for passengers to ride, and a dormitory is attached to the office on the mountain for tourists to eat and stay.

News

Procedures for Private Universities to Submit Documents to the Ministry 18

Ministry of Education Circular Transmitted by Provincial and Municipal Departments and Bureaus

The Ministry of Education previously received a request from the Shanghai Special City Education Bureau to order all private universities to submit documents to the Ministry through their local departments and bureaus. The Ministry considered the request to be essential and yesterday ordered all provincial and municipal departments and bureaus to transmit it to their subordinate private schools for compliance. The original order is transcribed below: According to the Shanghai Special City Education Bureau's report, Article 21 of the Regulations for Private Schools stipulates that the establishment of a private school should be submitted by the competent Education Department or Special City Education Bureau to the Ministry of Education for transmission. The transmission should include a detailed investigation and comments for review. According to the terms of the article, the competent department and the detailed investigation and comments during transmission mean that private universities are also subject to the management of the local departments and bureaus. Since the establishment documents are transmitted by the competent department, other documents should also be handled in the same way. Recently, private universities have often directly submitted reports or requests to the Ministry, which not only violates the regulations but also makes it difficult for the competent departments and bureaus to understand the school's operation status. There is a sense of isolation in matters such as guidance for further education and guidance for visits. When the Director attended the National Education Conference in Beijing, he personally reported to the Minister, who approved that all documents submitted to the Ministry by private universities and all documents given to private universities by the Ministry should be transmitted by the departments and bureaus for examination. It is requested that all private universities be ordered to comply. According to the previous situation, Article 1910 of the Ministry's decree in the 18th year has stipulated that the board of directors of private vocational schools or specialized schools that have been established should report the items listed in Article 13 of the Regulations for Private Schools to the provincial and municipal education administrative agencies for periodic reporting. According to the previous situation, the investigation is essential. In the future, all private vocational schools or specialized schools that have been established or are in the process of closure should submit or request the Ministry for review, except for urgent matters that cannot wait for transmission, or request for tax-free passports and study abroad certificates that are not related to educational administration. All matters should be transmitted by the local provincial and municipal education administrative agencies to avoid isolation and facilitate examination. In addition to the order, the department is ordered to comply and transmit it to all established private vocational schools or specialized schools under its jurisdiction for compliance. This order.

Ministry of Education 19

Reiterates the Registration Method for Academic Organizations

The Ministry of Education recently issued an order to the Education Departments and Bureaus of all provinces and cities, stating that the Ministry has issued the Regulations for Education Administrative Agencies to Manage Academic Organizations and ordered the Education Departments and Bureaus of all provinces and cities to quickly submit the current registration status of academic organizations within their jurisdiction to the Ministry. It has been found that the Education Departments and Bureaus of all provinces and cities have not uniformly submitted this current status. The items listed in the table of local academic organizations submitted by those who have submitted are not fully consistent with the Regulations for Education Administrative Agencies to Manage Academic Organizations previously issued by the Ministry, which is insufficient for statistics. In the future, regardless of whether it has been reported or not, all academic organizations within the jurisdiction should be transferred in accordance with Articles 3 and 4 of the aforementioned Regulations ((3) The establishment of an academic organization must be initiated by the initiators who draft the regulations and submit them to the provincial or special municipal education administrative agency for approval. The regulations should be recorded in accordance with the provisions of Article 47 of the General Principles of the Civil Code: A purpose, B name, C appointment and removal of directors, D conditions and procedures for convening a meeting and methods of proof, E members' capital contribution and the acquisition and loss of member qualifications (4) After the establishment of an academic organization, the following items, together with all regulations and rules, should be registered with the provincial or special municipal education administrative agency where it is located: A address of the office, B name, age, native place, academic qualifications, and occupation of the directors, C detailed items of assets, funds, or other income, D name, age, native place, and academic qualifications of the members. After registration, if there are changes in the regulations and rules and the above-mentioned items A, B, and C, they should be reported to the Ministry for record at any time) to be submitted to the Ministry for record and statistics.

Zhejiang Province Handling 20

Literacy Campaign Publicity Precautions

The following are the publicity precautions for carrying out the literacy campaign in various counties and cities in Zhejiang Province: 1. The publicity campaign for carrying out the literacy movement in various counties and cities should pay attention to the following purposes: (1) to enable the public to recognize the need for literacy (2) to enable the public to understand the methods of seeking literacy (3) to arouse the public's interest in literacy (4) to arouse sympathy and support for the plan to popularize literacy education 2. The publicity campaign for carrying out the literacy movement in various counties and cities should pay attention to the following principles: (1) The publicity must strive to cover the entire area and not be limited to one corner. (2) The publicity method must strive to adapt to the general public to make it effective and not just be extravagant. (3) Effectively contact local public education institutions. (4) Strive to save on expenditures and not waste funds. 3. The duties of the literacy movement publicity committee in each county and city shall focus on planning and implementing the publicity matters of the literacy movement in the respective counties and cities. However, the plan and method for implementing literacy education shall also be studied and discussed, and shall be submitted to the relevant agencies for selection and implementation. 4. Each county and city may, depending on the circumstances, organize a district literacy movement publicity committee to plan and implement the publicity matters of the literacy movement in the respective districts. 5. After the establishment of the literacy movement publicity committee in each county and city, the county and city government should submit the establishment process, the list of committee members, and the simple regulations of the meeting to the education department for record. 6. When each county and city submits the list of members of the literacy movement publicity committee, it must include the following items: (A) Name (B) Representing agency or group (C) The position held in this agency or group 7. If there are any changes in the regulations and list of members of the literacy movement publicity committee in each county and city, they should be reported for record at any time. 8. The literacy movement publicity committee in each county and city should discuss and determine the annual plan and budget before the beginning of the year, and submit it to the county and city government for approval and include it in the local education general plan and general budget for submission to the education department for record. 9. Literacy movement publicity week will be held once a year throughout the province at the same time. The date and method will be decided by the Provincial Literacy Movement Publicity Committee, and the Education Department will issue an announcement for implementation. The publicity day will be determined by each county and city separately. 10. The publicity materials for the literacy movement in each county and city, in addition to being printed and distributed by the Provincial Literacy Movement Publicity Committee, will be printed and distributed by the Literacy Movement Publicity Committee of each county and city as appropriate. 11. The literacy movement publicity materials compiled by each county and city should be submitted to the education department for review at any time. 12. The Literacy Movement Publicity Committee in each county and city shall prepare an implementation report and final account after the end of the year and send it to the county and city government to be included in the general education implementation report and final account for submission to the Education Department for review.

Ministry Order on Compiling Mandatory Education Statistics

The Ministry of Education believes that the four types of Jiangsu Province's compulsory education statistics tables prepared by the Joint Office for Compulsory Education in Jiangsu Province are precise and commendable, and specifically orders the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities to refer to them and imitate them. The order reads:

According to Qin Fengxiang, the standing committee member of the Joint Office for the Preparation of Compulsory Education in Jiangsu Province, the four types of compulsory education statistics tables in Jiangsu Province have been submitted to the ministry. After investigation, the tables are precise. In addition to the instructions and orders, the tables are inspected and sent to the department for reference and imitation. This order includes one copy of the following tables: Statistics of Compulsory Education in Jiangsu Province, Statistics of Elementary School Teacher Qualifications in Jiangsu Province, Statistics of the Number of Children in Primary Schools in Jiangsu Province in Jiangsu Province in Recent Years, and Statistics of Elementary School Expenditures in Jiangsu Province in Jiangsu Province in Recent Years.

Ministry Order for Universities to Establish Library Courses

The Ministry of Education ordered national universities to adopt library regulations in accordance with the articles submitted by the China Library Association, which are not without merit.

According to the China Library Association, it submitted articles prepared in accordance with the resolution of the first annual meeting in January of the eighteenth year, requesting adoption and implementation. After investigation, the library business is an urgent matter for educational construction. Now that various places have successively established this special talent, there is an increasing sense of lack. The association's statement that it attaches importance to library professionals is not without merit. In addition to the separate instructions and orders, a copy of the original presentation and the original approval are sent to the school, requesting that it add library science courses or a library science department within the Department of Literature or the Department of Education, so as to cultivate this special talent for application.

Guangdong Education Department's Summer Education Administration Outline

(4) Yi Lu

7. (Education Statistics) A. Compile education statistics for the 17th year; B. Compile secondary education statistics for the first period of the 18th year. In terms of administration, education statistics are the standard for all facilities and plans. In terms of academics, they are the basis for studying the rise and fall of education. However, the concept of statistics is weak in various counties and cities, and statistics are regarded as unimportant. Therefore, the department's letters urging the reporting of statistics are no less than repeated orders and requests, but those who urge still urge, and those who do not report still do not report. The reason is that local soldiers and bandits have lost their files, and bandits are rampant and difficult to investigate. Others say that they have no economic resources and it is difficult to fill out the report. Among the above reasons, some are true, but those who do not understand the meaning of statistics and lack statistical talents take the opportunity to delay. The department plans to compile education statistics for the 17th year and education statistics for the first semester of the 18th year in order. If the counties and cities still ignore them, in addition to submitting a special case to the provincial government for the promulgation of disciplinary measures, it is planned to compile them using [partial] analysis methods according to the nature of schools at all levels in order to complete them as scheduled.

8. (Others) A. Continue to send inspectors to set off. Inspectors will still be divided into seven districts and dispatched in accordance with the previous method. The focus of this period is on qualitative improvement and using sufficient time to direct provincial schools. B. Compile Guangdong's current education laws and regulations. It has been included in the plan for the previous period, and it is now planned to urge its speedy compilation for reference and examination. C. Compile a summary of provincial schools. It has been included in the plan for the previous period, and it is now planned to urge its speedy compilation for reference and examination. D. Improve and ban student hostels throughout the province. The regulations for banning student hostels and the regulations for registering student hostels were formulated and promulgated by former Director Huang, but they have not been effectively implemented. As for former Director Xu, the department formulated various implementation measures and handed them over to the Guangzhou Municipal Public Security Bureau to be responsible for handling them without success. The purpose of banning student hostels is to protect students living outside the school and general youths to prevent them from being infected with bad habits. However, banning student hostels from a negative perspective is laborious and ineffective. It is now planned to start from a positive perspective and convene the training directors of secondary and higher schools to discuss the management of students living outside the school, and then revise the various chapters and regulations for banning student hostels in order to make them practical. E. Compile the school calendar for the 19th year. Now that the Ministry of Education has issued an order to revise the regulations on the school year, semester, and holidays of schools, we should immediately comply with the provisions of Article 10, Paragraph 1 of the regulations and compile and publish the school calendars of primary and secondary schools in the 19th year separately. The provincial industrial college and private specialized schools above the specialized level have compiled the school calendar for the 19th year for schools above the specialized level and sent two copies to the department before April 20 for submission to the Ministry of Education for record. F. Improve school physical education. School physical education should pay attention to the average development of the body and mind of all students, strengthen physical fitness, be lively in spirit, and cultivate habits of observing discipline and harmony. Therefore, the types of sports should be in line with this purpose in order to promote physical education. After investigating the schools in the province, although they can do their best to promote physical education, they mostly focus on cultivating competitive athletes and ignore ordinary exercises. Not only does this violate the original intention of school physical education, but also the efficiency of sports will be reduced. We should find ways to improve it in order to improve national health. It is planned to formulate other measures during this period to ensure that all students can receive ordinary exercises in order to improve the efficiency of physical education.

9. (Research on New Education) A. The Provincial First Normal School, the First Middle School, and the Girls' Normal School are designated as experimental schools. The administrative plan for the pre-service period has been reported and should continue to be tested and assessed. B. Experimental Field for Dynamic Education. The Experimental Field for Dynamic Education, which was established by former Director Xu, has been reported in the administrative plan and should continue to be tested and assessed. C. Research on Provisional Standards for the Curriculum. The Ministry of Education ordered former Director Xu to establish a meeting for research and should continue to urge its progress and report the results of the research to the Ministry of Education for inspection and approval as scheduled. (End)

Local

Joint Graduation Ceremony

The Shanghai Municipal Secondary Schools held a joint ceremony yesterday, hosted by the Municipal Education Bureau. Because the schools are located in different places and there is no auditorium, the ceremony was held in two places, the Penglai Theater in Nanshi and the Central Auditorium in Beishi. The ceremony in Nanshi was held from 9:00 am to 12:00 pm, with the participation of more than 20 schools and more than 1,000 people. The ceremony in Beishi was held from 2:00 pm to 4:00 pm, with the participation of more than 40 schools and more than 1,000 people. Director Chen, the chairman, performed the ceremony as scheduled.

Chairman's Address

Today is the first joint graduation ceremony of secondary schools in Shanghai. The main reasons for holding the joint ceremony are: (1) to avoid the tediousness of holding separate ceremonies (2) to enable graduates to develop group training (3) to enable graduates to have a more profound impression. This graduation ceremony is not only a grand joint event, but also more honored after the examination. The reason why the Education Bureau has the examination is also briefly described. Examination is a good system that has existed in our country since ancient times. Unfortunately, it was used by emperors to confine the tools of bookworms, which led to the burying of talents and the decline of morale. In principle, it also praises the examination, so it is listed as one of the civil rights. We have found abuses in past school exams. On the student side, they usually study hard, but when it comes to exams, they only know to ask the teacher for the scope. On the teacher side, in order to maintain personal achievements and reputation, they also give students hints in advance. This is not only a great concern for culture, but also a guide to the destruction of the nation. If we want to remedy and correct it, there is no other way than the examination. This is the beginning of our country and the time is short, so there are many shortcomings. We only seek to progress gradually and achieve perfection. Before the examination, there were supporters and opponents. We only have to overcome all difficulties and carry it out. Therefore, those who participate in the ceremony today feel more happy, and I think the students feel the same. After graduation, the paths are mostly to further education and employment. I would like to offer some humble opinions to you. Those of you who are going to work, society is a high-temperature melting pot, and Shanghai is even more so. You should be wary. In school, mistakes can be forgiven. In society, if there is any impropriety, criticism and scolding will follow. The best way to deal with society is to be patient. Be patient with all difficulties. What everyone should pay attention to is that there are always good opportunities in society. Do not miss them. However, difficulties come with opportunities. You still need to work hard to achieve success. Those of you who are going to further education, do you know how precious and difficult it is to be able to further education today? Not to mention those who cannot study today, there are many blind people who do not know how to read. There are even more people who have no food, no clothes, and no shelter. You can finish middle school and go on to further education. How should you encourage yourself so that you can be worthy of yourself, your family, and the country? The country spends huge sums of money on education to create good talents for the country. You should always realize that the country, society, and all people without clothes, food, and shelter have high expectations for you. You must work hard to live up to their expectations. Hard work is sincerity. I dare say that those who can be sincere in their studies will surely succeed. There is also something to tell you. The worst phenomenon in society today is the development of personal desires without regard for group discipline. Therefore, the bad academic style has reached its peak. Those who further their education should correct their mistakes in the future, and those who are employed must always respect group discipline and restrain personal desires. The future of the nation will have new hope. After the speech, Xu Peihuang, the representative of the mayor, issued graduation certificates and the director issued certificates of merit.

Mayor's Representative's Address

The mayor could not come due to business and asked me to represent him in participating in the joint graduation ceremony. Your results on this examination are very good and commendable. The two words "seeking knowledge" are not easy to say at present. Shanghai has a population of 3 million, which is about 30,000 households based on 10 people per household. If there is one middle school student in every 10 households, there should be 30,000 people. Now there are only 3,000 people, which is only one in a thousand. Your opportunities can be said to be very good, but your responsibilities are also very heavy. The chairman has already spoken about the bad academic style. No country in the world is like China, which is a shame for our country. Those who further their education should encourage themselves. The responsibilities of those who are employed are even more important than those who further their education. In Shanghai, one middle school student in a thousand people represents a thousand people. European and American education is also based on middle school, so middle school students are the basic organization of the country. You must be self-disciplined in society.

I would like to give you two words: "Pay attention." Learning is endless. You must not forget to learn after you are employed. Learning does not have to be in school. Do not be complacent and advance with the times. I encourage you.

Party Representative's Address

Mr. Huang Zaoxiong of Nanshi briefly said that this graduation is different from the past because of the examination. Academics are broad, so those who further their education should continue their future, and those who are employed should not give up their studies immediately, etc. Mr. Xu Yefu of Beishi briefly said that graduation is a period of transition to further education and social life, which is very important. Those who further their education should see the importance of saving the country by studying clearly. Studying without forgetting to save the country means studying to prepare for saving the country in the future. In the past, many students misunderstood and moved a lot of study time to saving the country, which not only wasted valuable time, but also caused young people with shallow experience and immature knowledge and unclear intentions to go astray. Therefore, in the future, we should recognize that serving the society is the most important thing, not to be discouraged and not to be complacent. It is easy to be discouraged when entering society from school. We should work hard to achieve hope. Discouragement is useless.

Principal's Address

Mr. Pan Gongzhan, the principal of Junyi Middle School, the representative of the principals in Nanshi, said briefly that middle school is the most important in the process of school. Although primary school is the foundation, its age is young and its knowledge is not yet fully developed. Middle school is different. On the one hand, it is the foundation of university, and on the other hand, it is a good citizen of the country, so its importance is known. Therefore, the soundness of the country will depend on the development of secondary education in China. What China needs now is (1) to never forget that I am a citizen of China, a member of the Chinese nation, and a good citizen with Chinese national characteristics (2) a good citizen who is honest, persevering, hardworking, patient, studies hard, cultivates morality, exercises physically, and has group discipline. This should be what you should reflect on. Since secondary education is so important, the responsibilities of principals and teachers are of course important, but students should also pay attention to it, etc. Principal Wang Xiaoying of Cimuwu Middle School said briefly (1) those who further their education should know that they are receiving secondary education and then receiving higher education to build China (2) those who are employed should transform the bad society and must not be melted by the bad society, etc. Principal Tang Naikang of Beizhong Middle School delivered a speech in Beishi.

Finally, the students answered. The representatives of Nanshi are Jingye and Minli, and the representatives of Beishi are Wang Jue of Daxia Affiliated Middle School and Shen Jiayuan of Jianzhong.

It was also said that there was much discussion during the meal regarding the school's future development.

Alumni Association of the School of Law General Assembly 32

Re-electing Executive Committee Members

The Shanghai School of Law Alumni Association convened its third general membership meeting at 3 PM in the new campus building of the alma mater in Jiangwan Road. At the same time, it elected executive committee members. Over three hundred people were present, including Wu Kaixian, Tao Baichuan, Du Gang, He Yuanming, Mao Yun, Jiang Jiemin, and Wang Youlin. Chairman Zhang Wenbo and Secretary Geng Boyang conducted the proceedings according to protocol. First, the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, followed by He Yuanming's report on the financial income and expenditure of the past year, along with the distribution of mimeographed balance sheets. Then, discussion began on the following: (1) Wu Kaixian proposed that the alma mater's library is currently being expanded, and the association should donate relevant books as a memento (Resolution): Donate a large collection of books worth over one thousand yuan, and entrust the Executive Committee to handle it. (2) He Yuanming proposed that because Zhang Wenbo, a classmate and director of the alma mater's affiliated high school, has resigned due to circumstances, the successor should be nominated by the association to the alma mater's authorities to seek and appoint someone from among the alumni in order to develop the alma mater's school affairs (Resolution): Passed. (3) He Yuanming proposed that the association should send representatives to participate in the alma mater's board of directors meetings and school affairs meetings to make suggestions (Resolution): Passed. (4) Mao Yun proposed that the Executive Committee of the association should report the status of the alma mater to all members at any time in the future (Resolution): Passed. (5) He Yuanming proposed that the association should send a letter to the alma mater authorities to add several school board members who are knowledgeable, have great character, and are enthusiastic about school affairs in order to develop the alma mater (Resolution): Passed. (5) (6) (7) (8) (9) Omitted for brevity. After the discussion was completed, the election of executive committee members resulted in Wu Kaixian, Tao Baichuan, Du Gang, He Yuanming, Mao Yun, Zhang Wenbo, etc., being elected as executive committee members, and Jiang Jiemin, etc., being elected as alternate executive committee members. After the election, the committee members immediately held their first executive committee meeting to discuss the distribution of duties. As a result, Wu Kaixian was named Standing Committee Member, Zhang Wenbo was named Documentation Committee Member, He Yuanming was named Accounting Committee Member, Tao Baichuan and Du Gang were named Communication Committee Members, Mao Yun was named Editorial Committee Member, and Li Zheng, Hong Junpei, and Ding Yao were named Investigation Committee Members.

All Sectors Support the Government 36

To Recover Concession Telephone Rights

Yu Qiaqing and Others Convene Meeting Yesterday

Since receiving a telegram from Minister of Communications Wang Boqun, requesting support from the Shanghai business community leader Yu Qiaqing and others for the government's recovery of telephone rights in the concessions, and to broadly publicize the matter in order to achieve the goal of recovery, a meeting was convened at 2:00 PM yesterday (the 25th) at the Hong Kong Road Banking Club to discuss measures with leaders from all sectors. Those in attendance included Yu Qiaqing, Zhao Jinqing, Wu Yunzhai, Qian Xinzhi, Yuan Ludeng, Li Zuyu, Xu Xinliu, Wang Zhiwei, Hu Yunqiu, etc. Yu Qiaqing was elected as chairman, and Wang Zhiwei as secretary. After the chairman explained the purpose of convening the meeting, the attendees spoke in detail and explored the matter, resolving the following two points: (1) The Shanghai Special Municipality Business Community Consolidation Committee and the Shanghai Concession Taxpayers Association will publish an announcement in the newspapers, asking the Chinese shareholders of the China and Foreign Telephone Company to abstain from attending the company's special shareholders meeting on the 27th of this month to show their determination to support national sovereignty and laws. (2) Those present at today's meeting will jointly telegraph Minister Wang of the Ministry of Communications to reply. The meeting adjourned at approximately 3:00 PM. The announcement and telegram reply are recorded below:

Announcement to Chinese Shareholders of the Shanghai China and Foreign Telephone Company: Regarding the matter of announcement, the telephone business exclusively operated by the Shanghai China and Foreign Telephone Company in the Shanghai Special District (i.e., the Public Concession and the French Concession), the National Government Ministry of Communications, in order to complete our national sovereignty and enforce national laws, has decided to recover the franchise rights and purchase the company's assets at a fair price. Therefore, this announcement is specifically published to all Chinese shareholders of the Shanghai China and Foreign Telephone Company. All Chinese shareholders shall abstain from attending the shareholders meeting convened by the company on the 27th of this month to show their determination to support national sovereignty and laws. Please take note. Shanghai Business Community Consolidation Committee, Shanghai Concession Taxpayers Association, June 26, 1920.

Reply to Minister Wang of the Ministry of Communications, Nanjing: Upon receiving your telegram regarding the China and Foreign Telephone Company's unauthorized sale to foreign merchants and the concession authorities' unauthorized granting of franchise rights for new companies' public utilities, which is of great importance to national sovereignty, all Chinese people are strongly opposed. Therefore, we have unanimously resolved to resist attending the company's special shareholders meeting on the 27th of this month to express our active opposition. We await the government's serious negotiations to achieve the goal of recovery. Yu Qiaqing, Qian Xinzhi, Zhao Jinqing, Hu Yunqiu, Li Zuyu, Wang Zhiwei, etc.

The Municipal Council's 37

Two-Percent Extra Tax

To Be Abolished from July 1st

Announcement by the Chinese Taxpayers Association

The Shanghai Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association issued an announcement yesterday, stating: Regarding the announcement of the abolition of the two-percent extra tax, the Public Concession Municipal Council has been levying a two-percent extra tax since July 1, 1927, which caused disputes due to the lack of consent from the Chinese taxpayers. After mediation, it was paid under protest for three years. Now, according to the Municipal Council's budget for this year, the two-percent extra tax will be abolished from July 1st of this year. Therefore, the announcement is made that all Chinese taxpayers in the Public Concession shall pay the Municipal Council's municipal tax (commonly known as police tax) from July 1st of this year according to the rates before June 30, 1927. Please take note. Shanghai Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association (Address: No. 4 Hong Kong Road, June 26, 1930)

End of the Pharmaceutical Industry Labor Strike 38

Months of Dispute

Peacefully Resolved

Qualified Applicants Employed by the Trade Association Through Lottery

The Shanghai National Medicine Trade Association previously received a letter from the Business Consolidation Committee, selecting 50 names from the list of 101 unemployed pharmaceutical workers sent by the Citizens Training Association to be introduced to the association to be forwarded to the pharmaceutical employers for allocation and employment, along with a paper of the selected 50 names. After receiving the letter, the association immediately convened a follow-up meeting yesterday to properly resolve the matter. After discussion, the following measures were resolved: (1) How should the service store numbers and jobs of the 50 unemployed workers be allocated fairly? It was resolved to use a lottery method, and the names of the 50 people were written on paper rolls, and the counter duties were separated. The managers of the employing stores drew lots in public. (2) The 50 people who have been drawn should properly find a shop guarantee according to commercial practices and then enter the shop to work. It was resolved to ask the Business Consolidation Committee to send a letter to the Citizens Training Association to order the trade union to quickly send the guarantee form of the 50 people to the association before the 30th of this month to comply with the procedures. (3) The unemployed workers who were forcibly placed by the trade union and forced to sign an acknowledgment should leave the shop on a fixed date. It was resolved to ask the Business Consolidation Committee to send a letter to the Citizens Training Association to strictly order the trade union to withdraw the number of people as soon as possible and not to delay. The 50 people who have been drawn will enter the shop to work on a fixed date after the previous batch has left the shop and prepared the procedures. (4) Among the 50 people, one named Gao Bingsheng has already found a job, so the association should select another person to fill the quota. It was resolved to use Zheng Hengshan to fill the quota. (5) The 51 unqualified unemployed workers have been given severance pay and dismissed, and their trade union membership certificates should be revoked. The severance pay received should be signed for by the recipient and sent to the association for record. It was resolved to transfer the matter to the Business Consolidation Committee and ask the Citizens Training Association to comply. (6) How should the salary of the 50 people who are employed this time be determined? It was resolved to issue the minimum amount of the originally set salary for each store, and to send a letter to the Business Consolidation Committee to forward it to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and the Citizens Training Association for reference. (7) The employment of 50 people in each store this time is an exception. The employees of the store should not use this as a request for promotion and salary calculation. It was resolved to ask the Business Consolidation Committee to forward a letter to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and the Citizens Training Association for reference. The meeting adjourned at 7:00 PM.

Declaration of the Pharmaceutical Workers' Support Association to End

The Shanghai Trade Unions Aid Pharmaceutical Workers' Union Support Association declared its closure yesterday as the issue of the pharmaceutical workers' employment has been resolved, and published a closing statement as follows: In recent months, the local pharmaceutical workers have been resisting the employers' refusal to employ unemployed workers and oppressing trade unions, causing a major labor strike that has almost become unmanageable. This is a well-known event. We workers, standing on the same front, are very disgusted with the various actions of the pharmaceutical employers. In order to help fellow workers on the same front and to promote the awareness of the stubborn employers, we have organized a Pharmaceutical Workers' Support Association to provide economic and material support to the pharmaceutical workers who are oppressed by the employers and to be their strong backing. The purpose of our association is very simple: to help unemployed workers in order to promote the employers to accept their reasonable demands. The reason for the establishment of our association is also a manifestation of the workers' class being greatly stimulated and realizing the great unity and fighting against the evil forces. During the past working period, the workers have been able to do their best to help, so that the pharmaceutical workers have received a lot of spiritual and material comfort and help. The facts of this incident tell us that the Shanghai workers' class has indeed become aware. The pharmaceutical workers' strike has now been resolved peacefully, and the responsibilities and missions of our association can also be concluded. Our association convened a plenary committee meeting on June 20 to discuss the closing matters. All accounts have been reviewed by the appointed commissioner, and will be published in the newspapers as soon as the review is completed. The remaining funds have also been appointed to responsible personnel. Those trade unions that have already recognized the amount but have not paid will also be invalidated. From now on, our association announces its closure. The workers in the pharmaceutical industry were able to achieve considerable success this time, and the help of the city's workers is indelible. This is the benefit of our workers' great unity. In the future, if there are any stubborn employers who undermine labor-management cooperation and exploit workers' interests, the city's workers must unite and fight against them, otherwise it will not be enough to show the great power of the workers. Our great and beloved workers, please pay attention to this declaration.
